posted:Posted May 20, 2024
msg:Considering the location, transportation, service quality, catering quality, and hygiene & safety, I chose a branded hotel at the same price, just to save worry and feel at ease. As it turns out, I made the right choice!
Transportation: 30 minutes from Dali Airport and 10 minutes from the high-speed rail station. Even if you order takeout, you can enjoy the route advantages of both the ancient city and the city (there are more varieties than the homestays in Haixi and Haidong)
In addition, the hotel is opposite Dali Port! Super convenient!
Facilities and hygiene: New hotel, everything is guaranteed. I have to praise the windows, they are so clean! Watching the sunrise in the room in the morning (although the location is remote, the morning glow is also beautiful) is completely ok!
Service quality: The housekeeper Miss Solar always responds positively from the perspective of guest needs. Very trustworthy~ The room arranged has a direct view of Erhai Lake, and you can see Cangshan Mountain (although the clouds are thick in May) and Erhai Lake~ Very satisfied~ The front desk and other waiters are also very polite and enthusiastic~
Food quality: The two best meals I had in Dali were at Pullman Hotel... Well, Dali Scenic Area is a food desert... Even the pizza ordered from Pizza Hut is so bad that it's incredible. You must try the cross-bridge rice noodles in Pullman's Chinese restaurant! The soup is delicious, the rice noodles are smooth, and the ingredients are fresh and rich! ! ! The Japanese skewers at the Starry Sky Bar on the last day are also very distinctive (Yunnan-style grilled skewers). PS: Starry Sky Bar requires reservations, and it is best to ask the chef if the reservation time is available, otherwise the meal may take a while.
Finally, I strongly recommend Pullman's cross-bridge rice noodles and lake view rooms again! ! !

b. The air conditioner is very warm and there is a bathtub. You can ask the guest room for bath bags and bath salts. Toiletries are non-disposable, and you can also ask for one-time use from the guest room, which is very convenient and fast.

Service: I thought that many tourists would be too busy during the peak period, but in fact the experience was very good. Starry Sky Bar: The Starry Sky Bar has a good environment, a good a**osphere, and a good view. The bartender is very good. He can perfectly prepare a glass of wine with complicated requirements. I am very satisfied. It is recommended to let the bartender do his best when ordering wine. Special and worth it.

Chinese restaurant: I dined in the restaurant twice, and I ordered dishes for dinner. The taste is normal Yunnan cuisine (but we are not very used to it), and the food is served slowly. tasty! But the speed of serving the food was really too slow. The waiter sent a stack of beef to express his apology, but hoped that it would be better to serve the rice noodles faster.

To sum up: I am very satisfied overall, it is a relatively satisfactory journey, and I will be willing to stay in Pullman again when I come to Dali.

msg:During the Spring Festival, I took my children and the elderly to Dali to bask in the sun. Due to personal hotel preferences, I abandoned the many Internet celebrity homestays in Dali and stayed at the newly opened Pullman Hotel for 6 days and 5 nights. After in-depth experience, I felt as follows:

üçÉ Environment:

It is located in Xiaguan District, next to the Xingsheng Bridge in Dali City (that is, a special bridge), and opposite to Dali Port, so the view of the hotel's seaside room is very overbearing!
Frankly speaking, the hardware of Pullman is not luxurious. Compared with other Pullmans, the lobby of this hotel gives people a bright feeling. There is a beautiful spiral staircase on one side, and the lounge area where guests check in is also quite distinctive. The perfume smells pretty good too.
In terms of other facilities, the gym and swimming pool are quite satisfactory. The only downside is that there is no children's playground. If families with children choose a house hotel, it will be a little troublesome.
Overall, the hardware of this Pullman in Dali is not bad.

Room:

Our group booked two rooms, and we were lucky to be upgraded to an executive sea view room when we checked in (but did not enjoy executive courtesy). Although the housekeeper coco invited us to the executive lounge for afternoon tea, but due to personal travel reasons Come on, that's for a later story.

The decoration style of the whole room is modern and simple wooden style. Due to the new opening, all the facilities are very new. The sea-facing room type can see Dali Port and Erhai Lake completely unobstructed. Sitting on the bay window beside the bed, watching It is very pleasant to see Erhai Lake.

Room amenities are Pullman's own brand, and tea and capsule coffee are replenished daily. Children's equipment is also fully prepared, which is quite parent-child friendly

It is worth mentioning that Pullman's sleep system, you can choose the right pillow by yourself, call the guest room, and you can quickly get it.

Meals:

When staying in a hotel, we usually experience hotel meals. In addition to the normal daily breakfast, there will be afternoon tea, lounge and dinner if the opportunity arises.
Let‚Äôs talk about breakfast first: Pullman‚Äôs breakfast can be regarded as quite satisfactory. There are certain choices of Chinese and Western styles. When you sit down, you will ask if you want tea or coffee, which is quite professional. However, the actual eatability of the breakfast category is not so high, especially our resident guests, who will feel a little boring later.
This time, the afternoon tea and lounge were not experienced because of our personal itinerary, but we went to the high-altitude starry sky bar. Since smoking is allowed indoors, we also chose to give up with children intelligently, so we did not experience it.
For the dinner, we have a buffet dinner. The most eye-catching dishes are the seafood and western pastries. The overall taste is quite satisfactory, and it may be a bit boring for people who don't like seafood.

üîîService:

The last thing to say is the hotel service, which is the most dazzling part of this stay. Before checking in, the colleagues in the executive lounge called us to confirm the itinerary, and we successfully enjoyed the hotel's airport pick-up service. There was welcome tea at check-in, coco in the executive lounge also sent us to the room, and wechat sent Dali's travel reference, helping us with the service throughout the whole process, which was very heart-warming.
It needs to be mentioned that during our stay, we encountered a water pipe leak in the room with a burst water pipe upstairs. We called the front desk and quickly gave us an empty room opposite us for us to go to rest. We also apologized the next day, and we could see the hotel. For the emphasis on guest experience, this deserves a lot of praise.

Overall, the Pullman selection this time was quite successful! It can be said that this Dali Pullman is a flagship.
